	name = USA_dem_rep_loc

	   localization_key = USA_dems_reps_tt2
	}
	text = {
	   localization_key = ""
	}
}

#trigger tooltips - only visible if mentioned var is in government array

defined_text = { 
	name = mutual_Neutral_conservatism_20_tt_loc

	text = { 
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 1 } 
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
			}
		}
	   localization_key = mutual_Neutral_conservatism_20_tt2
	}
	text = {
	   localization_key = ""
	}
}

#show if over threshold

defined_text = {
	name = Western_Autocracy_cannot_invite

	text = { 
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^4 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^5 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^8 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^9 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^11 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^19 > election_threshold }
				check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^21 > election_threshold }
			}
		}
	   localization_key = Western_Autocracy_invite_extra
	}
	text = {
	   localization_key = ""
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = Western_Autocracy_valid

	text = { trigger = { check_variable = { party_pop_elect_array^0 > election_threshold } }
	   localization_key = coal_Party_0
	}
	text = {
	   localization_key = ""
	}
}
